Like all Boston pianos, it features the patented Octagrip&trade; pinblock and the maple rim, offering the highest level of playing comfort for pianists and amateur artists as well as institutions.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><ul><li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Finish: polished black<\/li><li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Length: 215cm<\/li><li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Width: 155cm<\/li><li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Weight: 404kg<\/li><\/ul><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">The Boston piano designed by Steinway &ndash; long unrivaled in its class and unmatched in value &ndash; has been significantly enhanced with the introduction of the new Performance Edition. The Boston Performance Edition features improvements in materials, specification, and performance that have never been seen before in the mid-price range.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">A maple inner rim, otherwise found in only the finest pianos, increases structural integrity and improves the tone by isolating the soundboard. The patented Octagrip&trade; pinblock provides a smoother pin turn and more consistent pin torque, leading to more precise tuning.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">When you purchase a Boston piano, you have the option of returning it for 100% of the original purchase price if you invest in a new Steinway grand piano within ten years.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br /><div class=\"video-wrap product\"><iframe allowfullscreen=\"\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"360\" src=\"//www.youtube.com/embed/X7FRVARlt28?feature=player_embedded\" width=\"640\"><\/iframe><\/div><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Technical details and features<\/strong><br />All Boston grand pianos have duplex scaling &ndash; one of the most famous inventions by Steinway &amp; Sons, which provides a full, balanced and especially long-lasting tone. The duplex systems installed in the cast iron plate provide a rich array of overtones and harmonic diversity.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">In order to meet the highest quality standards, only the finest Sitka spruce is used to build the Boston&rsquo;s soundboard &ndash; wood with a straight grain and a defined minimum number of annual rings per centimeter. Based on the design of Steinway &amp; Sons in 1936, the Boston soundboard is not uniformly thick, but tapers toward the ends. This allows it to vibrate more freely and generate a fuller sound.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">In addition, each Boston grand piano features extended housing, no matter what its size. This is an innovation by Steinway &amp; Sons that makes it possible to widen the rear of the housing. Compared to other instruments of the same length, Boston grand pianos therefore have a much larger soundboard. For example, a Boston grand piano measuring 178 cm can be fitted with a soundboard that would normally be used for a standard grand piano measuring 189 cm in length.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">A range of Steinway patents and designs were incorporated into the construction of Boston at the outset. In 2009, the introduction of the revised Boston Performance Edition heralded a number of extraordinary innovations, two of which are of particular importance. The rim of the Boston clearly bears the genetic fingerprint of Steinway &amp; Sons. While the outer rim consists of several layers of mahogany, only maple is used for the inner rim. As a result, the housing is not only more stable, but it also offers a much more pleasant sound &ndash; the fundamental goal of the Steinway system. In efforts to optimize the new generation of Boston grand pianos, engineers came up with the patented Octagrip pinboard, whose design is based on the Hexagrip pinboard principle conceived by Steinway &amp; Sons. This feature can only be found on Boston pianos.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Fine woods provide the Boston pianos with a beautiful shell: walnut and mahogany will impress those who want an alternative to traditional black or white &ndash; after all, Boston pianos should provide their owners with joy for the eyes as well as the ears.<\/p>","active":true,"price":"40000.00","old_price":"50825.01","discount":21,"from":"2019-10-15T21:00:00.000Z","till":"2019-10-29T22:00:00.000Z","image":1541763362,"search_index":"'black' 'boston' 'flīģelis' 'gp' 'grand' 'melns' 'pe' 'piano'","tags":[],"partner_id":"33570","partner_uri":"http://attrademusic.lv/lv/precu-katalogs/taustini/akustiskas-klavieres/fligeli/boston-gp-215-pe-fligelis-(melns)/gp-215-ehp/3002945/1/prod/33570","partner_categories":["Akustiskās klavieres","Flīģeļi"],"info":null,"info_lv":null,"info_ru":null,"name_index":"'black' 'boston' 'flīģelis' 'gp' 'grand' 'melns' 'pe' 'piano'","warning":null,"partner_category":94614,"type_name":null,"discount_value":"10825.01","notability":6.28734540057731,"run":"2019-10-22T22:29:48.838Z","slug":"boston-gp-215-pe-fligelis-melns-","processed":"2019-10-22T22:43:16.539Z","online":true,"offline":true,"visible":true,"salidzini":false,"imagesize":0,"aliexpress":false,"currency":"EUR","admitad":false,"characteristic_product":null,"icecat_product":null,"name_en":"Boston GP-215 PE flīģelis (melns)","description_en":"<p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Pateicoties 215 cm garumam, &scaron;is instruments ir lielākais Boston flīģeļu klāsta modelis. This reduced string tension, along with a tapered soundboard, creates longer sustain, and a more singing quality in the tone (as well as longer piano life). A wealth of other engineering enhancements, including optimal placement of ribs, braces, and bridges, also contribute to the Boston&rsquo;s superior tone and greater stability.<br /><br />The Boston grand piano offers a larger soundboard in comparison to other pianos of the same length, due to its innovative &ldquo;wide tail&rdquo; design. This wider construction of the case means that a 5&#39; 10&quot; Boston grand has the same soundboard area as a typical 6&#39; 2&quot; grand piano, creating the power, richness, and feel of playing a much larger piano.<br /><br />Each Boston piano soundboard is crafted of Sitka spruce, long proven to be the most resonant material available. Boston soundboards are solid (not laminated) and precisely tapered, which allows them to vibrate more freely. In conjunction with a number of special technologies &mdash; unique patents of&nbsp;STEINWAY &amp; SONS&nbsp;&mdash; the result is a powerful, sustained tone.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Dimensions<\/strong><\/p><ul><li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Length: 178 cm (5&#39; 10&quot;)<\/li><li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Width: 151 cm (59&frac34;&quot;)<\/li><li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Height: 102 cm (40&quot;)<\/li><li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Net Weight: 333 kg (733 lb)<\/li><\/ul><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Encasement<\/strong><\/p><ul><li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Cabinet Style: Classic<\/li><li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Finish: High Polish White<\/li><li style=\"text-align: justify;\">Hardware: Solid brass &mdash; polished and lacquered.<\/li><\/ul><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Specifications<\/strong><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Rim<\/strong><br />Hard Rock Maple inner rim -- this is the foundation of the Boston&rsquo;s tone. Besides providing superior structural integrity to the piano, it enhances tone by being a rock hard foundation for the soundboard. A Maple rim is found only in the finest pianoss. Continuous bent rim. 11 outer rim laminations, 17 inner rim laminations. 23 mm (⅞&quot;) outer rim width, 38 mm (1&frac12;&quot;) inner rim width.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Braces<\/strong><br />Radiating braces solidify the piano&rsquo;s structure. Their triangular layout provides more support than parallel designs. This rigid system improves &nbsp;tuning stability and soundboard crown retention, and lengthens&nbsp;&nbsp;3 braces.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Pinblock<\/strong><br />Octagrip pinblock made of 11 layers of Hard Rock Maple &mdash; glued in different grain angles of 60 degrees &mdash; affording the tuning pins greater stability under tension and enabling the piano to stay in tune longer.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Soundboard<\/strong><br />Close and straight-grained solid (not laminated) Sitka Spruce. Minimum 3 annual growth rings per cm (minimum 8 per inch). Tapered from treble to bass, allowing a greater freedom of movement in the bass, and stiffness in the treble, thereby creating a richer and more lasting tonal response.&nbsp;Tapered from 8 mm to 6 mm. Vibrating area: 1.30 m2&nbsp;(2,020 in2)<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Ribs<\/strong><br />Made from durable spruce to assure strong and constant support of the strings bearing down on the soundboard. Ribs are fully let-in to the inner rim to support the important soundboard crown and prevent the piano from losing its tone. Number of ribs: 11<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Bridge<\/strong><br />Treble: Vertically laminated (alternating maple and mahogany) with a solid maple cap, curved to fit the crown of the soundboard. Bass: Solid maple mounted to cantilevered base.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Scale<\/strong><br />Overstrung; combination of agraffe, with front and rear duplex. Rescaled bass and treble for lower tension scale for increased sustain, better tone clarity, and deeper clearer bass.&nbsp;17,445 kg (38,460 lb) tension.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Plate<\/strong><br />Cast from grey iron, bronze-painted and lacquered. Based on the design of Steinway &amp; Sons in 1936, the Boston soundboard is not uniformly thick, but tapers toward the ends. This allows it to vibrate more freely and generate a fuller sound.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">In addition, each Boston grand piano features extended housing, no matter what its size. This is an innovation by Steinway &amp; Sons that makes it possible to widen the rear of the housing. Compared to other instruments of the same length, Boston grand pianos therefore have a much larger soundboard. For example, a Boston grand piano measuring 178 cm can be fitted with a soundboard that would normally be used for a standard grand piano measuring 189 cm in length.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">A range of Steinway patents and designs were incorporated into the construction of Boston at the outset. In 2009, the introduction of the revised Boston Performance Edition heralded a number of extraordinary innovations, two of which are of particular importance. The rim of the Boston clearly bears the genetic fingerprint of Steinway &amp; Sons. While the outer rim consists of several layers of mahogany, only maple is used for the inner rim. As a result, the housing is not only more stable, but it also offers a much more pleasant sound &ndash; the fundamental goal of the Steinway system. In efforts to optimize the new generation of Boston grand pianos, engineers came up with the patented Octagrip pinboard, whose design is based on the Hexagrip pinboard principle conceived by Steinway &amp; Sons. This feature can only be found on Boston pianos.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Fine woods provide the Boston pianos with a beautiful shell: walnut and mahogany will impress those who want an alternative to traditional black or white &ndash; Ashley has written dozens of number one singles and has over three hundred songs recorded by several prominent artists. Here, we get a glimpse into Ashley&rsquo;s process and we learn why he thinks the Genos is a terrific songwriting companion.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"video-wrap product\"><iframe allowfullscreen=\"\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"343\" src=\"//www.youtube.com/embed/kQbN3HztjAA\" width=\"610\"><\/iframe><\/div><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Beth Nielsen Chapman on songwriting and the Yamaha Genos Digital Workstation<\/strong><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Genos, the latest flagship Digital Workstation from Yamaha, is an incredibly inspiring songwriting tool as well as a powerful performance and studio instrument. Yamaha reached out to Nashville hit songwriter Beth Nielsen Chapman and asked her to work with Genos for a while and let us know what she thought about the instrument. Beth has written for dozens of pop and country stars including Faith Hill, Willie Nelson, and Waylon Jennings, and was recently inducted into the songwriting Hall of Fame. Here, Beth describes her passion for writing and talks to us about how the Genos inspires her and makes her process both easier and quicker.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Features<\/strong><\/p><div id=\"d1126372\"><div><div><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><u>The best sound quality ever on a Digital Workstation<\/u><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><\/div><\/div><\/div><div id=\"d1097369\"><div><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Powered by specially developed Yamaha technology, the sonic quality of every Voice in Genos is beyond any other Digital Workstation you&#39;ve ever played. Everything you hear, whether it be the beautiful CFX piano, the lush Kino Strings or the punchy Revo!Drums, will blow you away!<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><u>-AEM (Articulation Element Modeling)<\/u><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">This technology simulates the subtle nuances and performance characteristics of musical instruments. When you play, Genos automatically chooses appropriate samples in real time, according to what and how you play. Samples are smoothly joined and articulated, just as they would naturally occur on an acoustic instrument.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><u>-C7 Grand Piano<\/u><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">For the first time in any Yamaha product, the Genos features our newly sampled C7 Grand Piano Voice. It is great match with Pop/Rock/Jazz and other music, and is the piano of choice for many recording studios around the world.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><\/div><div id=\"d1126375\"><div><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"https://usa.yamaha.com/files/revo%20drum_400x357_1460eddb2aea21a520c3b8625d84bfbe.jpg\" /><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><u>-Revo!Drum/SFX<\/u><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Revo!Drum Voices recreate the authentic sound of drums. Even when playing the same key multiple times, the sound is always of a different nuance, making it incredibly natural and realistic.<\/p><\/div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><\/div><div id=\"d1097370\"><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Content<\/strong><\/p><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Whether you create or perform music, you need to be inspired by your instrument. Genos features a diverse range of content, including 1,710 instrument Voices, 550 accompaniment Styles, 216 arpeggios and more.<\/p><\/div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><\/div><div id=\"d1097371\"><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Effects<\/strong><\/p><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">From Reverb to Distortion, Rotary Speaker to Compressor, Genos boasts unprecedented DSP power. 28 insert effects can be routed freely, making Genos an incredibly versatile production tool.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Using the same VCM technology as professional Yamaha mixing consoles, Genos has the tools to create the perfect sound. Not only do the effects sound great, they look great too&mdash;with a stunning graphical user interface.<\/p><\/div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><div id=\"d1097372\"><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Vocal Harmony &amp; Synth Vocoder<\/strong><\/p><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">You can automatically apply various Vocal Harmony effects to your voice as you sing, or you can use the Synth Vocoder to craft the unique characteristics of your voice onto synthesizer and other sounds.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><\/div><\/div><div id=\"d1097502\"><div><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"https://usa.yamaha.com/files/F3D76BA1AC644513A9F638FDB185F676_12074_400x240_814228b0f5f8ee056143251db5b21e35.jpg\" />&nbsp;<img alt=\"\" src=\"https://usa.yamaha.com/files/8A1F7995380C40EBAF893C1124542AF1_12074_400x240_a299809b2dd254c40c420018a86b0929.jpg\" /><\/p><\/div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><\/div><div id=\"d1097373\"><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Expand your music<\/strong><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"https://usa.yamaha.com/files/Yamaha-Expansion-Manager_400x199_cf6b793f7d692153ab5f7d17408b4a4f.jpg\" /><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">You can continually expand the onboard content of your Genos by creating and installing your own custom or purchased Packs. The scope of possibilities for new sounds and styles is virtually unlimited.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><u>-YEM (Yamaha Expansion Manager)<\/u><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">YEM is PC/Mac software designed to manage the Expansion contents for Yamaha keyboards.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><u>-Integrated Flash Memory<\/u><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Genos includes 1.8GB of user flash memory with high speed reading/writing for your own Voices.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><\/div><\/div><div id=\"d1126380\"><div><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"https://usa.yamaha.com/files/yem_image_400x228_128ec8eaeb02f4129ebe80ed1662d992.jpg\" /><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><u>-Extra USB memory slot for data storage<\/u><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Genos has three USB TO DEVICE ports (one on the panel, one on the back side, one on under the instrument) for you to keep the data.<\/p><\/div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><\/div><div id=\"d1097410\"><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Control Your Music<\/strong><\/p><\/div><\/div><div id=\"d1097374\"><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Intuitive and fast control<\/strong><\/p><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Genos features an intuitive interface for music making and sound creation.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><u>-Touch Screen<\/u><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Select and change parameters directly with the new 9&quot; colour touch screen.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><u>-Assignable buttons<\/u><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">While performing, you often need to act fast to access certain features. Choose from a range of functions to set to the 6+1 assignable panel buttons and with just a single touch, you can instantly recall your desired function.<\/p><\/div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><div id=\"d1097376\"><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Style Engine<\/strong><\/p><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Genos features a variety of rhythmic backing patterns and accompaniments (called &ldquo;Styles&rdquo;) in variety of different musical genres. Styles feature sophisticated patterns to inspire your creativity. You have the ideas, and Genos will react to them.<\/p><\/div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><div id=\"d1097377\"><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Registration Memory<\/strong><\/p><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">The Registration Memory function allows you to save (or &ldquo;register&rdquo;) virtually all panel settings to a Registration Memory button, and then instantly recall your custom panel settings by simply pressing a single button.<\/p><\/div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><\/div><div id=\"d1097411\"><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Shaping Your Idea<\/strong><\/p><\/div><\/div><div id=\"d1097378\"><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Turn great ideas into reality<\/strong><\/p><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Start from the original idea of a song, pick an instrument Voice and Style of your choice. For more complex arrangements, Multi Recording features a fully functional 16-track MIDI sequencer with realtime and steptime functionality.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">When you are happy with your recording, it can be stored to the internal User Drive or saved to USB Memory for easy sharing.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><u>- Digital output<\/u><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">The new S/PDIF Digital output can be connected to compatible studio equipment or home theatre to output audio from Genos without any loss in quality.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><\/div><\/div><div id=\"d1097504\"><div><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"https://usa.yamaha.com/files/209D09E640BC4851AF2AC6ABBC38E119_12074_400x240_de2c787e56bd02d6ff320b35ff8453dd.jpg\" />&nbsp;<img alt=\"\" src=\"https://usa.yamaha.com/files/Features_Shaping-Your-Idea_2_400x240_76e8f9d223f5d3e033cc83641b776391.jpg\" /><\/p><\/div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><\/div><\/div><div id=\"d1097380\"><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Arpeggio<\/strong><\/p><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Genos has 216 Arpeggios to enhance your performance. There are a variety of arpeggio types, some are straight forward instrument arpeggios, others recreate strumming guitar effects and controller arpeggios automate Live Control by adjusting sound filters in realtime as you perform.<\/p><\/div><\/div><div id=\"d1097381\"><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>High quality keyboard action<\/strong><\/p><div><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">The FSX keyboard features a premium action with aftertouch. The keys are created in a high-precision manufacturing process for an incredibly durable keybed, enhanced key stability and &quot;fast&quot; action. piano experience, and our new HP pianos are among the most exciting yet. The HP piano philosophy is all about bringing the sound and performance of a concert-class piano into your home, with a choice of cabinet styles, colors, and speaker systems to suit your lifestyle. The premium HP605 is powered by the latest version of our acclaimed SuperNATURAL Piano Modeling technology, along with a unique keyboard that blends wood and molded materials for great feel and durability. The HP605 connects via&nbsp;Bluetooth&reg; technology to your smartphone or tablet so you can hear your music-making apps or online piano lessons through the powerful six-speaker sound system - your kids will love it too as it makes learning piano fun. And even though it&rsquo;s compact, the classically-styled HP605 will definitely make a big impact in your home especially with a choice of finishes including polished ebony, contemporary rosewood, and contemporary black or white.<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"video-wrap product\"><iframe allowfullscreen=\"\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"343\" src=\"//www.youtube.com/embed/GPJP65EMK50\" width=\"610\"><\/iframe><\/div><\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Features<\/strong><\/p><ul><li><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Uses the latest SuperNATURAL Piano Modeling technology instead of conventional sampling, for a far richer, more detailed piano sound<\/p><\/li><li><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Acoustic Projection system, with six speakers that work together to recreate the deep, rich sound field of an acoustic piano<\/p><\/li><li><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Headphones 3D Ambience technology for natural, realistic sound when practicing on headphones<\/p><\/li><li><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Authentic grand piano touch from the new PHA-50 (Progressive Hammer Action with Escapement) keyboard combining the appearance and feel of wood with the durability of modern materials<\/p><\/li><li><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Connect your smartphone or tablet via&nbsp;Bluetooth&nbsp;technology and practice piano with audio from apps routed through the piano speakers<\/p><\/li><li><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Also includes a large, versatile selection of non-piano sounds such as strings, brass, organ, and many others<\/p><\/li><li><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">25 registrations for storing favorite sound setups, including layers and splits; registration groups can be backed up to a USB memory stick<\/p><\/li><li><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Imposing piano cabinet with a compact footprint perfect for smaller spaces<\/p><\/li><li><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Four premium finishes; authentic polished ebony, contemporary rosewood and contemporary black or white<\/p><\/li><\/ul><p style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><div><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>SuperNATURAL Piano Modeling for a Rich, Living Piano Sound<\/strong><\/p><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">Press a key on most digital pianos and you&rsquo;ll hear a recording of a piano note. But a SuperNATURAL Piano works differently, using the latest modeling technology to recreate, rather than replay, the sound. The unique modeling process spans the entire sound creation process of a typical piano including the combination of notes played, their resonance and the way in which the piano&rsquo;s many elements interact with each other. The result is a rich, complex sound - complete with overtones - that actually changes in response to the way you play; something impossible to achieve when a piano uses samples. It&rsquo;s the difference between just listening back to a recording or actually being there yourself.<\/p><\/div><div><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Recreating the Rich, Deep Sound of an Acoustic Grand Piano<\/strong><\/p><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">Roland&rsquo;s Acoustic Projection speaker system reproduces the rich sound of an acoustic grand piano. The HP605 houses a three-way, six-speaker system, driven by a powerful four-channel amplifier and each section fulfils a specific role in delivering superior piano tone. The powerful cabinet speakers produce the all-enveloping main piano sound, while the top-mounted spatial speakers reproduce the resonance of the piano&rsquo;s frame. Finally, the nearfield speakers project the sounds most likely to be noticed by the player, including dramatic, dynamic overtones and even the noise of the hammers as they hit the piano string. The increased height of the cabinet further enhances the richness of the sound.<\/p><\/div><div><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Grand Piano Sound Through Your Headphones<\/strong><\/p><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">One of the great advantages of a digital piano is the ability to play quietly with headphones. However, when used with headphones, some digital pianos simply switch the sound from the speakers to your ears. This is a missed opportunity as good headphones can provide remarkable clarity and detail when you&rsquo;re practicing. Roland pianos use Headphones 3D Ambience to optimize the audio so it sounds like it&rsquo;s coming from within the piano itself not through your headphones. You&rsquo;ll also be able to practice for extended periods of time without fatigue, any time of the day or night.<\/p><\/div><div><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>The Look and Feel of a Wooden Keyboard, Without the Drawbacks<\/strong><\/p><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">The wooden piano keyboards often found on acoustic pianos are attractive to look at and they feel solid and substantial under your fingers. But a completely wooden keyboard is not the best approach for a digital piano, as wooden keys need regular maintenance to keep them in the best condition. The HP605 has a new type of keyboard that blends wood and molded material for the best of both worlds; beautiful wooden sides give each key a familiar, rigid mass that feels just right to play, while the durable inner frame means you can enjoy your Roland piano every day for years to come without worrying about reliability. You can play it every night too - as our piano key construction also produces less of a &ldquo;thump&rdquo; noise when played.<\/p><\/div><div><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Plays Like an Acoustic Grand Piano<\/strong><\/p><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">It&rsquo;s not just the feel of the keys either; the way they move is also important. Each key has a stabilizing pin to ensure the vertical travel of the key is smooth and precise, avoiding the sideways key movement and noise experienced when playing glissandos on some pianos. Since the HP605 has our latest piano engine onboard, we also retuned the key sensing system to match it, ensuring that the sound and keyboard work in complete harmony for the ultimate piano experience. Finally, the keys share the look and feel of real ebony and ivory, and their moisture-absorbing properties mean your fingers won&rsquo;t slide off when playing.<\/p><\/div><div><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">&nbsp;<\/p><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Connect Your Smartphone or Tablet via&nbsp;Bluetooth&nbsp;technology - and Use Apps to Make Learning Easy<\/strong><\/p><p data-show=\"on-scroll\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">Today, people often play and learn the piano with the aid of smartphones and tablets. Using&nbsp;Bluetooth&nbsp;technology, the HP605 wirelessly connects to your mobile device, enabling you to take advantage of popular iOS/Android apps and online practice videos. Once connected, the audio is routed through the piano&rsquo;s internal speakers, or headphones if you prefer to practice in private. Then you can play along with your favorite artist and bands or practice with some of the very best piano teachers.
